4. C(C(HHH)C(HHH)C(HHH)O(C(HHH))) + Cl* = C*(O(C(C(HHH)C(HHH)C(HHH)))HH) + Cl(H) [HA]

528. C*(C(//OC(HHH))HH) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(C(//OC(HHH))HH))) [OA]

538. O(C(C(//OH)C(HHH)C(HHH))C(O(H)HH)) + H2O = C(C(O(H)//O)C(HHH)C(HHH)O(C(O(H)HH))) [HC]
